      <Math mode="display" tex="f_{N}(x)\sim 2^{2/3}\sqrt{\pi}\sum_{k=0}^{\infty}a_{k}\Phi_{k}(x)," text="f _ N * x similar-to 2 ^ (2 / 3) * square-root@(pi) * ((sum _ (k = 0)) ^ infinity)@(a _ k * Phi _ k * x)" xml:id="S0.E4.m1">
